  <script>
    function shouldShowAnnouncementBar() {
      try {
        if (!window.Static.SQUARESPACE_CONTEXT.showAnnouncementBar) {
          return false;
        }
        var localDataStr = localStorage.getItem('squarespace-announcement-bar');
        if (localDataStr && JSON.parse(localDataStr).closed) {
          return false;
        }
        return true;
      } catch(e) {
        console.error(e);
        return true;
      }
    }
    if (shouldShowAnnouncementBar()) {
      document.body.classList.add('announcement-bar-reserved-space');
    }
    //# sourceURL=reserveSpaceForAnnouncementBar.js
  </script>

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="sqsrte-small" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">Whether you are looking for a casual game with friends or rekindling a family rivalry… ForeVR Bowl has you covered! Explore 8 immersive lanes (The Moon, Tiki Hall, Atlantis and more!) and unlock 150+ unique bowling balls to find your perfect game. Climb the leaderboard and win weekly events and challenges. Choose from 1000s of songs on the YouTube-powered Jukebox. Bowling solo, online multiplayer and local pass-and-play will never be the same in VR!</p><p class="sqsrte-small" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"> Pick a side in 'Versus Mode' each week to win prizes for your team. Strike a pose with friends and document your Bowling Night fun with the brand new Selfie Cam. Search each hall for unlockable Hidden Balls.</p><p class="sqsrte-small" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>Price<br></strong>$19.99 USD</p>

        const firstSection = document.querySelector('.page-section');
        const header = document.querySelector('.header');
        const mobileOverlayNav = document.querySelector('.header-menu');
        const sectionBackground = firstSection ? firstSection.querySelector('.section-background') : null;
        const headerHeight = header ? header.getBoundingClientRect().height : 0;
        const firstSectionHasBackground = firstSection ? firstSection.className.indexOf('has-background') >= 0 : false;
        const isFirstSectionInset = firstSection ? firstSection.className.indexOf('background-width--inset') >= 0 : false;
        const isLayoutEngineSection = firstSection ? firstSection.className.indexOf('layout-engine-section') >= 0 : false;

        if (firstSection) {
          firstSection.style.paddingTop = headerHeight + 'px';
        }
        if (sectionBackground && isLayoutEngineSection) {
          if (isFirstSectionInset) {
            sectionBackground.style.top = headerHeight + 'px';
          } else {
            sectionBackground.style.top = '';
          }
        }
